Radio Weekly

Designing an Output Transformer

— Li Yuanqing

In either DC or AC circuits, the larger the external resistance, the greater the voltage obtained; the smaller the external resistance, the greater the current obtained. If you want to get the maximum power, then the external resistance must be equal to the internal resistance of the power source. Everyone who has studied electrical engineering probably knows this basic law.

The first diagram shows the wiring method of the output circuit of a new AC radio. The output point XX is connected to the voice coil L of the loudspeaker through an output transformer T. Most people think that the function of the transformer T is only to protect the voice coil of the loudspeaker, but in fact it also shoulders a more important mission: to increase the output power and obtain the maximum undistorted volume. (Maximum Undistortod Power) If you don't believe it, try omitting the transformer T and connect the voice coil L of the loudspeaker directly into the output circuit, and you will immediately see a significant impact on the volume and sound quality.

The reason is very simple: the resistance of the voice coil of an ordinary electric loudspeaker is probably only about ten ohms, but the screen resistance of an ordinary vacuum tube is as high as several thousand ohms. Since the difference between the two is so great, the output power is naturally pitifully small. The best way to remedy this is of course to find a way to increase the resistance of the voice coil of the loudspeaker, but this is not easy to do in practice. So, thinking on the other hand, we can only use a transformer to reduce the vacuum tube's screen resistance to a considerable value.

We know that in a transformer, the more turns the coil has, the greater the voltage and the more the resistance; conversely, the fewer turns the coil has, the smaller the voltage and the less the resistance. In this way, we can solve the above-mentioned difficulty by using a transformer with a suitable ratio.

The design of the ratio of a typical output transformer is generally calculated according to the following formula:

For example, in the first figure, V is a 45 powerful output vacuum tube with a screen resistance of about two thousand ohms, and L is the loudspeaker voice coil with a resistance of about ten ohms. According to the above formula, we get:

Transformer Ratio

That is, in the situation shown in the first figure, you must use a 14:1 output transformer to get the maximum output power.

In a receiver, only the output power is required to be as large as possible, and the sound quality is irrelevant. But in a radio, on the one hand, it is required to be able to get the maximum output power, and on the other hand, the distortion of the sound quality must also be taken into account. According to practical experience, the load resistance must be twice the screen resistance of the vacuum tube in order to get the maximum undistorted output power.

Therefore, in a radio, the above-mentioned output transformer ratio should be changed to:

Transformer Ratio

That is, in order to get the maximum undistorted output power, you must use a 20:1 output transformer.

When the external resistance is twice the internal resistance, the output power is about 11% smaller than when the external resistance is equal to the internal resistance. Usually, a quarter of the power reduction only results in a small decibel loss in volume. The human ear cannot easily detect a loss of only one-tenth of the power.

In short, when designing an output transformer, the resistance of the primary coil should be large rather than small. According to practical experience, even if the load resistance is five times greater than the screen resistance, the difference in volume compared to when the internal and external resistances are equal is only about two decibels. Ordinary people probably need a change of three decibels to be able to distinguish the volume. If the load resistance is smaller than the internal screen resistance, then not only will the output volume be reduced, but also serious distortion will occur in the sound quality.

Reviving Aging Vacuum Tubes

— RF

If a vacuum tube is used carelessly and the filament receives a higher than specified voltage, the filament may not burn out, but it will lose its ability to detect or amplify. Or, due to prolonged use, the filament may naturally age and no longer detect or amplify. Both of these can be revived, and after revival, they can still be used normally. The method is as follows:

(1) Pass a current that is about three-quarters higher than the specified filament voltage through the vacuum tube filament for a moment (for example, if the specified filament voltage of a 01A is 5 volts, you can pass a current of 8 volts through it. The shorter the energizing time, the better; otherwise, the vacuum tube may be burned out. Special attention must be paid to this point.) Then, pass a current according to the specified voltage through the filament for about two or three hours; then it can be used normally.

(2) This method is newly discovered and has a very good effect. (The author had a No. 1109 vacuum tube, which was greatly weakened due to accidental connection to high-voltage B battery, and the sound was as low as a mosquito's buzz, so it was abandoned for several years. The other day, while checking old items, I saw it and treated it with this method, and now it can be used normally, with effectiveness no less than a new vacuum tube.) The method is to use a blowtorch, the flame temperature of which is about 1200 degrees Celsius. (If there is no blowtorch, you can use a gasoline stove, a Bunsen burner used for chemical experiments, etc. A regular alcohol lamp can also be used reluctantly.) Slowly insert the top of the glass bulb of the damaged vacuum tube into the flame of the blowtorch, first gently heating it, and then applying more heat. Do not rush when doing this, so as to avoid the glass bulb bursting due to sudden heat. When the mercury layer on the vacuum tube bulb is partially vaporized by the heat, you should stop heating and let it cool down slowly. After cooling, its ability is no less than a new vacuum tube.

In general, seven or eight out of ten vacuum tubes whose filaments have not broken but are ineffective can be revived by one of the above two methods. With a few tens of minutes of effort, a vacuum tube that would otherwise be useless can be continued to be used. If a broken vacuum tube can save a few dollars, it will also slightly reduce the leakage of national wealth, so I have described it in detail above.

Reviving Broken-Filament Vacuum Tubes

— Chen Xianwen

Everyone knows that the vacuum tube is the heart of the radio, so you have to take care of it. However, even with a little carelessness, this omnipotent heart can lose its function. This causes a great economic loss to amateur researchers. To remedy this loss, one way is to prevent the misfortune from happening, and the other is to deal with the situation after the unfortunate event has occurred.

Everyone probably already knows how to prevent misfortune from happening (such as installing fuses in the B battery, etc.), so there is no need to say more now. What I want to talk about now is how to deal with it after the misfortune has happened. The method of treatment varies depending on the degree of damage. Now I will introduce the methods of treatment to everyone:

The method of reviving vacuum tubes whose filaments have not burned out has already been introduced above, but in the past, when a vacuum tube filament broke, this tube became useless. I have always wanted to revive them, but there was no safe method. Only now have I achieved success using the principle of electric welding. The equipment used is very simple, only an ordinary doorbell transformer and an interrupter (very similar to the vibrating device of a doorbell). Its circuit connection is shown in Figure 1. Its function is: when the intermittent current generated by the interrupter is sent into the primary coil (low-voltage coil) of the transformer, a high-voltage current is generated in its secondary coil (high-voltage coil). Then, this high-voltage current is sent into the filament of the vacuum tube, and an electric spark is generated at the break in the filament. When the electric spark is generated, strong heat is produced, which firmly welds the break in the filament. I have used this method to repair nine vacuum tubes for myself and my friends. Because this method can still be used in practice, I am announcing it to introduce it to everyone!

Note:

(A) The above method cannot be used to revive filaments that are no longer in their original position, or when the break in the filament is too far away.

(B) When welding vacuum tubes with higher filament current, the output current of the transformer secondary must also be larger, otherwise only electric sparks can be seen at the filament break and there is no possibility of welding. However, if welding filaments with lower filament current (such as RCA 201 and UX199, etc.), there is no need for a larger current. If it is too large, you will not get good results. Because the filament current is small, its diameter must be thin, and its heat of fusion is small.

(C) The current input to the primary of the transformer can be direct current (DC) or alternating current (AC). However, it should be noted that: when using DC, there is no need for a larger voltage (a 12-volt battery is sufficient). When using AC, because the inductive reactance of the transformer and interrupter is very large, a higher voltage is required to be effective, about 40 volts.

(D) If the primary input of the transformer is alternating current, a large spark will be found in the spark gap (the interrupter). Not only will the surface of the vibrating reed be easily burned, but also because there is a discharge current passing through it, its intermittent current will not show a drastic change (such as from zero to maximum, or maximum to zero), so the output voltage of the transformer secondary will be greatly reduced. To avoid this drawback, a fixed capacitor (0.1 Mfd or 0.2 Mfd) can be connected in parallel at the spark gap, as shown by the dashed line in Figure 1.

The Process of Manufacturing Fixed Resistors (Continued)

— Ke Ming

The dried strips are now ready to undergo an important journey, that is, the white heat of a large furnace. These large furnaces have temperature controllers that can produce a constant temperature of over 2500 degrees Fahrenheit around the narrow holes in the furnace, through which the resistance strips are slowly passing. The embryonic resistors remain in this high heat for nearly an hour, and the degree of heat is such that the alloy supporting the outside of the belt is also burned to white heat.

The clay casing and the central resistance material are now fused into an inseparable, hard-as-stone resistor. Ordinary fire cannot harm it in the slightest, moisture cannot penetrate its dense ceramic, and ordinary overloads do not cause its permanent resistance to change.

The long strip of resistors is cut into appropriate lengths by a fast-rotating wheel, and then each section is sent to the laboratory for the first material test.

Many of the cut resistors are hung in a steel box, leaving only the ends exposed. The steel box is then moved along a chain in front of two nozzles that spray a layer of pure copper on the heads of the resistors to provide a base for subsequent welding. This metal spray requires an oxyacetylene flame (with a high temperature of 2400 degrees Celsius). The copper wire is fed into this flame at a steady pace, and the copper wire evaporates in this high heat and sprays onto the heads of the resistors, where it immediately hardens into a uniform coating. In this way, the resistor can last for a long time.

The resistors are then tested again and sorted according to value, and then, through complex mechanisms, the connecting wires are wound and welded. No corrosive solder is used, and they are inspected again before being coated with the appropriate colors according to the standard color code. (End)

An Excellent Crystal Radio

— Chun Gang

Because crystal radios are more popular among the masses, there are many people who play with crystal radios. It is very interesting to spend a small amount of money and be able to enjoy high-class entertainment. Moreover, crystal radios do not cost electricity, and once they are made, they can be used forever. But they also have some shortcomings, namely poor selectivity and low volume. This is really a big problem for crystal radios. Because volume and selectivity are relative, good volume means poor selectivity; good selectivity means low volume, and the two cannot be combined. The crystal radio diagram above was published in an old foreign magazine a few years ago, but I only know the circuit and can't remember anything else. Recently, because a friend asked me to make a crystal radio, I chose this circuit, and the results were surprisingly good, almost as good as a one-tube radio. Although the antenna I used is very good, it is at least several times better than an ordinary double-loop crystal radio, so I am introducing it to everyone.

The coil is made in a rocker drum style (like a three-loop style). The outer tube has a diameter of three inches, and the inner tube has a diameter of two and a half inches. The outer tube is wound with 26 enameled wire for 50 turns, with a tap every five turns. If you want to be more precise, you can make a tap every three turns. The inner tube is wound with 28 enameled wire for 25 turns, and taps are made like the outer tube, but the taps of the inner tube do not need to be too long, as long as they can be turned into right angles. After it is made, connect the coil head of the outer tube to the coil end of the inner tube in series, so that it becomes a single rotatable coil. Connect the taps of the inner and outer coils to a tap switch respectively for separate adjustment. C2, which is drawn with a dashed line in the diagram, can be added or not. However, when you install it, you may want to add one to try and see what the difference is. In the diagram, C is 0.0005 Mfd, C is 0.0001 Mfd.

Small Experiences

The Frame of the Regeneration Coil Should Also Be Grounded

— Zhu Ziyuan

A friend of mine recently installed a one-tube radio. The coil was a spiderweb type, and the regeneration coil could be rotated in and out. After installation and testing, he found that the human body had a very strong influence. Later, he grounded the moving plate of the variable capacitor. When adjusting the wavelength, the human body's influence was indeed gone. But when he went to adjust the regeneration coil, the human body's influence was still there. When adjusting to the point where the vacuum tube was about to oscillate but had not yet oscillated, as soon as he let go of his hand, either the regenerative power weakened, or the headphones screamed wildly. After fiddling around for a long time, he suspected that the copper frame of the regeneration coil was to blame, so he connected a wire from the copper frame to the ground wire. The human body's influence was indeed gone, and it was very convenient to adjust both the wavelength and the regenerative power. Therefore, he knew that the copper frame of the regeneration coil should also be grounded.

Safe Screwdriver

— Qing

Ordinary screwdrivers only have insulation on the upper half, and the lower half is all conductive. If you are not careful when using them, a short circuit will occur, and vacuum tubes, coils, transformers, etc. may be burned. If you put a piece of rubber tubing of appropriate size and length on the conductor, you can avoid many unexpected losses.

Common Sense

— Huang Jiancun

(19) Overview of Vacuum Tubes (3)

(5) Structure of Pentodes: Pentodes are made by modifying the shortcomings of tetrodes. They can be divided into two major categories according to their different structures: American style and European style. (d) The above figure (A) is the common symbol for the American style, and (B) is the front view of its electrode configuration. The Radiotron brand sold on the market belongs to this type. (C) The figure is the common symbol for the European style, and (D) is the front view of its electrode configuration. The Philips brand belongs to this type. The difference in structure from tetrodes is that a third grid-like electrode is inserted between the screen grid and the plate, which is the so-called cathode grid. That is, it is composed of a filament F, a control grid CG, a screen grid SG, a cathode grid EG, and a plate P. This is a summary of the structure of pentodes.

(6) Operating Principle of Pentodes: As mentioned above, pentodes are made by modifying the shortcomings of tetrodes. The so-called shortcoming of tetrodes is the emission of secondary electrons. Originally, in tetrodes, if the plate voltage is lower than the screen grid voltage (a), another type of electron is emitted from the plate and flows into the screen grid. This phenomenon is called secondary emission. Therefore, a cathode grid is inserted into pentodes to eliminate the adverse phenomenon of secondary emission. The operating sequence is briefly described below:

If electricity is applied to the filament to heat it to a certain temperature, electrons are emitted from the filament. The speed of emission is increased by the presence of the screen grid SG, so the electrons pass through the control grid CG and the cathode grid EG and reach the plate P. Before the electrons reach the plate, although they have passed through the control grid and the screen grid, since the control grid is often supplied with a negative potential, there is no current flowing in the circuit of the control grid. Although the screen grid maintains a positive potential, the current flowing in the circuit of the screen grid is still very small, and with the help of the cathode grid, the secondary emission is eliminated. As a result, the plate current flowing in the plate circuit will inevitably increase greatly.

Spring and Autumn

Publicity

— Yongzi

People are really too clever. Clearly a number one coward, so afraid that they don't even dare to fight back, yet they insist on saying that they are honest and incorruptible, with nothing but the clothes on their backs. Clearly a man who has a weakness for women, who cannot be a Liu Xiahui or a Lu man, yet they will trot out the Rites of the Duke of Zhou, and the saying "of the three unfilial acts, having no heir is the greatest" as a big signboard. Clearly physically weaker than others, so scared at the sight of someone rolling up their sleeves that they have already retreated more than half of three "li", yet they insist on saying they love peace and don't want to engage with people. Clearly with no money in their pockets, they still pat their pockets when passing by a large store, saying, "I just don't like spending a lot of money to buy this kind of stuff."

These posturing words are obviously lies to anyone with a clear eye, words that cost nothing to say. Those who say words that cost nothing to say are naturally not upper-class figures, and are naturally scum of society. But in this day and age, lying has actually become a fashionable game. Just like calling sexual intercourse by the euphemistic phrase "the Rites of the Duke of Zhou," saying words that cost nothing is called "publicity."

Speaking of publicity, it's a big deal, because although foreign countries have it too, it's not something that we in China have had since ancient times, so it's a completely genuine import. Imports are naturally more popular than domestic goods, so whoever knows how to lie will be believed, and will not have their credibility swept away. If someone knows how to do publicity, even if the publicity is about things that could never be achieved even in a dream, they will surely make the reporters of major newspapers use the largest headlines to print it out, so that readers can read it, marvel and applaud, and shout their approval.

According to some, in this day and age, nothing can do without publicity. Something as small as hawking five-spice peanuts and fried tofu must be publicized to the fullest, to make people who don't want to buy them salivate between their teeth, or else you can't expect anyone to take out their wallet. It goes without saying that publicity is even more important for big things. Publicity can turn the dead into the living.

Pen, Skirt, and Gun

— Ji Yu

Pen refers to a penholder, skirt to a skirt sash, and gun to a gun barrel. To further explain the following text, as the ancients said, "My pen is like a knife," and "One worn-out pen is worth more than three thousand Mausers." These are all deceptive words. Perhaps they had some effect in the past, but now they are completely wrong.

No matter how sharp your pen is, how capable it is of turning the dead into the living and the living into the dead, it cannot match the magic power of a skirt sash. To have the advantage of a skirt sash, you must first have a few beautiful sisters to offer to wealthy old men, doing them favors. This can be done on a large scale or a small scale. Relying on this sash that pulls connections, you are guaranteed a stable job, enjoying inexhaustible benefits for life. As for the gun barrel, it is the most powerful thing in the world. Everyone fears it. With a gun barrel, you can arbitrarily execute journalists. If someone tries to impeach you, it's like splashing white water on a white wall. If you lose one territory, you can immediately get another elsewhere. The gun barrel is feared not only by those with pens but even by those with skirt sashes! So, the pen is the most useless thing!

Nowadays, those who make a living by talking, such as ballad singers, comedians, and movie stars, only need to use their mouths and hands, without needing a pen at all. If business is good, they can earn one, two, three, or four thousand a month. On the other hand, painters and calligraphers who rely on pen and ink can only earn three or four thousand a year. (Some famous painters who used to earn four or five thousand a year now only earn two thousand or more.) As for those who make a living by writing, it is even more difficult. Earning sixty or seventy yuan a month is already shocking. Compared to those who make a living by talking or embracing, the difference is enormous! They earn in one month what writers earn in six or seven years. Even if you work day and night, from night to dawn, without eating or sleeping, you still can't catch up with them!

Alas! Today, those who wield pen and ink have reached the end of their era! Perhaps in the near future, the worn-out pen will have no place to stand! I think:

Rather than being rejected in the future, it is better to recognize the situation early and prepare a trash can immediately. Those willing to abandon their pens should take them and throw them into the trash can together.

Four Company Commanders of the Northeast

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Nineteen: Wanting to Leave and Yet Longing to Stay, Recalling Past Events in the Same Car; Half Crying, Half Laughing, Leaning on a Pillow in a Sickly Autumn

However, Guizhi, while staying in the city, thought about her mother being alone at home and feeling lonely, so she insisted on returning after three days. Huang Manying saw her off at the tram station and then went back. Guizhi thought about how, the last time she and her mother came to the city, she had agreed to the Zhao family's marriage at the Huang's house. On the way home, she kept thinking about it. Self-Portrait Inscription

— Chuan Yizhi

Friends like to take photos. If the photos are good, they are framed or mounted in silver frames, repeatedly admired, and repeatedly caressed, because they cherish themselves and thus cherish their photos. As for me? I am like a tear in the vast Gobi Desert, considering myself too insignificant. If I want to see my sorrowful face, worn out by life, I can simply use a mirror coated with mercury on the back. There is no need for the troublesome process of having a photographer capture it with a lens and print it on paper. Fortunately, I have already "kicked the bucket." It's like a grain of sand blown into the air by the wind and then sinking into the sea—clean and simple. Why leave a photo behind for the world to waste and despise? As for hoping to leave an image on porcelain for my descendants to offer incense and worship before it for generations, that would be even more ridiculous than Huan Sima preparing a stone coffin for himself. Moreover, it would burden myself and my descendants. I am not some "national hero" or "revolutionary martyr" whose photo can be printed by a publishing company and sold as a profitable commodity. This has no meaning or benefit for me or anyone else. So, I fundamentally dislike these bothersome things.

The day before yesterday, Mr. Xinpu exceptionally used his own camera to take a two-and-a-half-inch full-body photo of me alone. Today it was finally developed. Looking at it, the stubbornly messy hair cannot hide the deep wrinkles on my forehead. These wrinkles are a record of a hard life, probably like the growth rings on a pine tree's cross-section, accumulating with the years! Two dark, inverted-eight-shaped eyebrows tightly cover two sunken eye sockets. The lower edges of the upper eyelids are each inlaid with a little shiny pupil, as if gazing intently at the direction of the final destination in the vast universe, or as if hinting to others at the difficulties of clearing thorns and the bitterness of one's own struggle failures. The cheeks are pathetically thin. The nose is high, and it doesn't seem unpleasant. The mouth is pursed shut as if containing anger. The ears only vaguely show a semi-elliptical shadow... This is not a suave, otherworldly appearance, nor is it a heroic posture full of spirit, and especially not a plump, happy, and long-lived face. It is the epitome of a genuine poor man whose courage has been broken by the demon's fangs and whose heart has been crushed by the boulders of life. Moreover, the small, square grid of the tall fence in the background symbolizes a net of troubles, further highlighting the outline of real life. I doubt if it is my own image. Looking in the mirror, I then believe that I am not what I used to be. If I have several years left, will I not resemble a skeleton? Alas! Premature aging, who is to blame?

I once compared myself to chopsticks, based on Yuan Zicai's poem about chopsticks. He said, "Laugh at you for being busy grabbing and sending food into other people's mouths; in a lifetime of sourness and saltiness, do you know what taste is?" Now, looking at this photo, I realize that being busy and getting nothing is like chopsticks, but even their quality of being strong and durable is far beyond my reach. Pitying myself in the "image," how can I not burst into tears!

Free Talk

On Translation and Introduction

— Mu Mutian

Fifteen years have passed since the May Fourth Movement. Since then, we have been gradually introducing Western literature to China. This time, almost twenty years, is not short. It should have been a considerable achievement in the introduction of Western literature. However, what is the actual situation?

None of Balzac's works have been fully translated into Chinese. None of Zola's novels have been fully translated into Chinese. Major works such as "The Decameron," "Don Quixote," "Gil Blas," "Satyricon," and "Les Misérables" either have only incomplete translations or, more often than not, don't even have incomplete translations. Apart from some Russian works translated indirectly by some people, there are even fewer works from other countries. Chinese translations not only fail to give a complete picture of Western literature, but also make it very difficult for young students to gain sufficient creative training from it. This is truly lamentable.

Indeed, introducing Western literature is not an easy task. In culturally backward China, introducing Western literature to a considerable extent cannot be achieved overnight. However, there are quite a few people in China capable of translating and introducing, and the past decade or so is not short. Yet, so few important works have been introduced. Although many reasons can be cited, the "comprador" attitude of many introducers is also a notable factor. Looking back, every friend has more or less committed this mistake.

By "comprador," I don't mean that the introducers and translators are "doing business." Rather, I mean that our introducers and translators have been doing their work under the influence of imperialism to varying degrees. Moreover, we are unconsciously affected by imperialism without even realizing it. One cannot help but lament "my unfortunate birth." In order to abandon the old tradition, we went to Europe to find new grain. But upon arriving in Europe, we were dazzled by a variety of colors and couldn't distinguish between genuine and fake goods. Imperialism showed us its kaleidoscope. We were captivated, our eyes were dazzled, and we said it was "beauty" and became "aesthetes." During the May Fourth Movement, we introduced Whitman and Wilde. Were we dazzled? When Hu Shi introduced Western novels, he didn't lead us to appreciate "The Decameron" or study Samuel Richardson and Fielding, but instead led us to know Kipling. What is the reason for this?

Of course, the social conditions in China also bear some responsibility for these tendencies. In China, the feudal remnants are too strong. Xu Zhimo's translation of Fouqué's "Undine" was not without reason. Balzac has not been translated into Chinese, while works by people like Labiche and Mendes have been translated to some extent, also for a reason. Because the cultural level of Chinese people is too low and their progressiveness is insufficient, imperialism has an opportunity to take advantage. Imperialists have unconsciously completed their task as "directors." We wanted to buy good goods, but as a result, we bought inferior goods.

The translation and introduction of Western literature are urgently needed in China now. But we want Western literary works to help the development of our own literature. During the Renaissance, European countries went to Italy to seek models. In the 18th century, English literature occupied a superior position in Europe. Naturally, China now needs to receive the influence of advanced countries. But we need to historically and objectively translate and introduce authentic works that can fully reflect society, and we should not let imperialist writers act as our "directors." We must always pay attention and be vigilant to prevent them from completing their task of "cultural aggression" through our translation and introduction. We must always be vigilant to prevent our translation and introduction from becoming "comprador"-like.

Actors and Dancers

— Sheng Fu

Actors and dancers are commonly referred to as "artists" in China. The only difference is that actors must put on a painted face when they appear on stage, hiding their true selves and posing as various characters to win applause from the audience. Dancers, on the other hand, are different. They don't hide themselves and sometimes even go so far as to strip naked, exposing their entire bodies. Although they inevitably put some powder on their legs, it doesn't detract from the true nature of their flesh. Therefore, spectators and critics often have overly harsh criticisms of the dancer's body, but they never see the hateful pockmarks and opium face on the leading male actor's face.

This is the secret of the painted face.

The Chinese have always been skilled in this art, and it is a genuine domestic product. Therefore, many clever people naturally want to cherish it and keep it as a national treasure.

As a result, painted faces are used in all kinds of grand occasions. Those who wear painted faces are naturally not all entertainers. Nor do they need to enter the Tianchan Stage. You can appreciate them everywhere.

Therefore, the scope of face critics has to be narrowed down to those who can't afford masks or completely naked dancers.

Recently, a "startling news" item was published in the newspaper, which attracted the attention of some people. The facts are roughly as follows:

At the Paris Dance Hall, dancers Yin Qiulian and Gao Lili were involved in a lawsuit over an assault case in the First Special District District Court. During the court hearing, Yin actually admitted to being a "Manchukuo" person. This surprised the defendant's lawyer "extremely," and many people denounced her in unison, almost stirring up the anti-traitor sentiment after the January 28th Incident.

This made me think that being a dancer is harder than being an actor, precisely because she can't be without a mask and is naked. If her profession had not been dancing but acting, she would have certainly been able to put on a show, saying, "She is a Manchukuo person, she is not a Manchukuo person," painting on a "unyielding," "no, no, unyielding," "master," and at the same time "slave" face.

But she doesn't know how to do this. She is actually regarded as a "slave," and even a "born" one. Even her parents feel quite dishonored. Moreover, the defendant's lawyer even said, "Manchukuo people certainly cannot be given legal protection," which also involves the risk that the assault case cannot be established, or even should bear the penalty for false accusation. It's really extremely unlucky.

However, I like her naked confession, not hiding in the least her willingness to be a slave of the Japanese Empire. Compared to some patriotic painted-face experts who swear oaths of love in front of people, but behind their backs fawn on foreign masters with servile faces, isn't she more lovable?

Disturbance

— Qing Nong

A disturbance arose in the communal courtyard this day.

In the early morning, the lovely autumn sun shone on the bungalows and low houses. Shortly after the "jazz music" had played, those large and small instruments, chamber pots, were still scattered in front of everyone's houses, sunbathing. The sister-in-law of "Wild Rose" upstairs, wearing a green-buttoned waistcoat, with disheveled hair, leaned on the iron railing, bent over, shaking her head, and brushing her teeth. The chaotic white toothpaste water dripped onto the stone slabs in front of the eaves downstairs with a crackling sound. The girl with two braids was drawing water by the well to wash vegetables first. The white-haired old woman in the low house had placed the washing board for washing clothes for others—the large wooden board that had become white and bright from washing clothes for so long—in front of the door and was about to lift the bucket and walk to the well to draw water. From the bend at the entrance came several burly men in black cloth gowns, including a foreigner in a Western suit. The children, who were excitedly half arguing and half playing marbles, stopped their active expressions when they saw this group of strangers, standing there in a daze.

"Foreign devil! What's the matter?" The little sister pointed her mouth at Little Shunzi's ear and asked softly. Little Shunzi looked carefully at the strangers, shook his head, and expressed that he didn't know.

"People from the yamen!" The girl with two braids quietly told the white-haired old woman who had walked to the well, with a surprised expression. As she spoke, she glanced at the "black cloth gowns."

The "black cloth gowns" confidently rushed into a room downstairs in the middle house. A surprised scream was heard from some auntie, followed by the shouts of the "black cloth gowns," "Don't move!"

The children stopped playing and gathered around. Little Shunzi squeezed into the room under the elbows of the "black cloth gowns" and was chased out with a shout. The little sister originally wanted to follow Little Shunzi in, but after hearing the shout, she couldn't help but be startled. Seeing Little Shunzi slip out and stick out his tongue, she was frightened, and her face changed from green to white.

The girl with two braids stood by the well, forgetting her work of washing vegetables, but the white-haired old woman didn't seem to feel anything and naturally drew water and washed clothes. The sister-in-law of "Wild Rose" upstairs squinted her eyes and watched, stopping her work of brushing her teeth, with the toothbrush still in her mouth, and the milky white toothpaste water dripping.

The people living in the middle house all gathered in the hall in front of the room being searched. The people from the houses on the left and right also ran out and stood outside their doors. However, the white-haired old man leisurely took out the spinning wheel from the low house, placed it in front of his door, sat down, and began his "violin solo"—the disturbance in the communal courtyard had nothing to do with him. They're searching for gambling! Big Sister's mother makes a living from this. Why don't they search her house? Looking around, Big Sister's mother isn't even in sight. Big Sister doesn't know where she's hiding.

The "black cloth gowns" shouted at the people gathered around watching the excitement, pushed them away, and walked out of the room. One of them was holding a wooden tray in his hand, filled with papers. That was probably the evidence. Some auntie followed them with a pale face.

"Go to the yamen!" The black cloth gowns said to her. She lowered her head and didn't say a word. She was probably imagining the humiliation of imprisonment and the pain of sitting in jail. Her eyes were moist.

The "black cloth gowns" left, and the auntie was gone. Only then did the people breathe a sigh of relief and speak, loudly.

"That's her old stash! I told her not to keep it, not to keep it, but she wouldn't listen!" Another auntie, who lived with that auntie, gestured and spoke to people.

Some people were sighing.

The children were already playing marbles on the dirt, and the white-haired old man's "violin solo" became more and more intense. The disturbance in the communal courtyard quickly subsided.

Two Brothers (Thirty-Nine)

— By Maupassant, Translated by Li Weike

They talked gently and intimately about ordinary things. The man's disposition had nothing extraordinary, but many gentle, tactful, and kind qualities. He was certainly a good friend to both of them, one of those good friends that one would never think twice about.

Now, many memories surged into Pierre's mind. Ma Raisa had seen him looking worried several times, guessed his poverty during his student days, and would voluntarily lend him money, perhaps several hundred francs. They had both forgotten about it, and he had never returned it. From this, it seemed that the man cared about his needs and had always loved him, always cared about him. Then... then why did he leave all his property to Jean? No, he had never shown more kindness to the younger brother than to the older brother, more concern for one than for the other, or outwardly more gentleness to one than to the other. Then... then... then he must have had a strong and secret reason to give everything to Jean—everything—and nothing to Pierre?

The more he thought about it, the more he revived the past few years, and the more he felt that Ma Raisa's differential treatment of the two brothers was inhuman and unbelievable.

An excruciating pain, an indescribable anguish that had penetrated deep into his chest, made his heart beat like a lock on a door being jiggled. The spring of this lock seemed to be broken, and blood flowed freely from there, shaking his heart restlessly.

So he said in a low voice, as if talking in a nightmare, "I must know for sure. God, I must know for sure."

Now he searched further, searching in the older days when his relatives were still living in Paris. But he couldn't remember their faces, which made his memories vague. He tried to remember whether Ma Raisa's hair was golden, chestnut, or black at that time. He couldn't remember after all. The man's last appearance, the old man's appearance, obliterated the appearances of other times. But he remembered that at that time he was thinner, his hands were very warm, and he often sent flowers, sending them frequently, because his father always said that sentence: "Sent flowers again! But you are a bit crazy, good friend, you will completely exhaust your money on roses."

Ma Raisa replied, "You don't care, I am happy to do this."

Suddenly, his mother's voice, the voice that smiled and said, "Thank you, my friend," pierced his mind. This voice was so clear, as if he could hear it. But she often said these two sentences, so it was so engraved in her son's memory!

From this, it seemed that Ma Raisa often sent flowers, he, a rich man, a gentleman, a customer, sent flowers to the old lady of this small shop, to the woman of the jewelry merchant in this cold village. Did he love her? If he did not love this woman, how could he have become friends with this merchant couple? He was an educated man with a rather refined nature. He and Pierre had talked countless times about poets and poems! He looked down on those authors who appeared in the guise of artists, but he greatly admired those authors who appeared in the guise of bourgeois. Doctors often couldn't help but smile at his actions, because in his opinion they were a bit silly. Now he realized that this affectionate and sentimental man had never been able to become his father's friend. His father was so practical, so vulgar, so stubborn. Poetry, in his view, was just equal to a kind of stupid thing.

Securities Swap: The Previous Bond Market Continued to Decline

Yesterday, at the Chinese Securities Exchange, the market was very busy with swaps between long and short positions due to the approaching end of the month for this month's futures. Market prices were quite abnormal, with more long positions being swapped, as it was still profitable to swap at the moment. If they could persist in swapping, they would eventually be successful, depending on their strength. The situation in Fujian Province did not change much. Although the central government and Guangdong Province were actively preparing for military action, they still hoped that Hu would arrive in Beijing and the matter could be resolved to avoid using force and causing hardship to the people. Therefore, there was still some hope for the future. The market situation was completely related to the number of chips. This phenomenon of squeezing long and short positions occurred every month's end. In the morning opening, the long positions knew that swapping was profitable, and many swapped to the near term, causing the market price to fall by a small amount of 0.03 to 0.04 yuan. Buyers mainly included numbers 3 and 53, followed by various others. Buyers saw a rebound of 0.03 to 0.04 yuan before the next round. After entering the market, the number of chips still exceeded demand, and the market turned weak again. In the afternoon round, the long positions swapped more actively. The difference between the near and far terms of demobilization was almost 1 yuan, indicating the enthusiasm of the long positions. Therefore, several types of futures for this month reached new lows. As a result, various other types also had stronger far terms than near terms. There was no need to be overly pessimistic about the future trend. Be cautious and prevent a sudden surge in the financial community, as their strength should not be underestimated. The market price ended with a continued decrease of 0.06 to 1 yuan, but the sharp drop of 1.8 yuan for this month's demobilization was somewhat excessive. The total transaction volume was 20,094,500 yuan, including 8,625,000 yuan for futures and salt tax, 2,875,000 yuan for demobilization, 2,045,000 yuan for 19 customs duties, 3,980,000 yuan for 20-roll 20 customs duties, and the rest ranged from tens of thousands to over 1 million.

New York Stock Market Still Difficult to Advance

Xinfeng Foreign Firm reported that the New York stock market on the 23rd saw a reverse trend in inflation in various markets. The dollar strengthened and then loosened by several points to 4 yuan. The rise in the dollar was due to the fixed official price of gold, the opposition to the government's monetary policy buying back dollars abroad, and reports that Canadians were selling securities in Britain and taking funds back to New York. The demand for dollars was thus greatly increased. Speculators are now awaiting President Roosevelt's speech tomorrow night. The demand for stocks is very low before the monetary situation is clear. Grains, silver, cotton, and other goods all fell. French and Belgian bonds also softened. Steel stocks turned firm at the last minute due to purchases by the automobile and railway industries. "Wheat, a few long positions were slightly closed, and new buyers were disappointed. Clarifying the monetary situation to restore credit is the fundamental condition for the market to recover. "Cotton, long positions have too many chips, and with the growing opposition to the government's monetary policy and no progress in business, the market is weak and about to fall. New buyers are watching the situation and not moving forward. The Financial Relief Agency buys gold at a price of 33.76 yuan per ounce, unchanged. The Dow Jones indices are listed below, closing prices compared to the previous day:

Thirty industrial stocks: 98.59, down 1.48

Therefore, new buyers feel very lacking. The current yarn market situation is unusually complex. Judging from the world situation, it is not appropriate to be overly optimistic.

Grain: Rumor of Tax Increase on Foreign Wheat to 4.5 Yuan; Standard Flour Moves Forward

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the market conditions for each month showed a preliminary consolidation followed by a jump. With foreign wheat quotations, Chicago continued to decrease by a small amount of 1.1 yuan, and Canada decreased by about 0.03 to 0.04 yuan. The appetite for actual sales was not as urgent as before. Therefore, the market atmosphere was flat at the opening. However, outside parties and speculative long positions in the market believed that the wheat source was not abundant and factories were reluctant to release stocks, there must be a major reason. Therefore, they still competed to buy first in each round, with a huge quantity, causing the market to rise step by step. Until the afternoon opening, there were no special circumstances at first, but later it was rumored that the government's tax increase on foreign wheat would increase to 4.5 customs gold (equivalent to about 0.07 to 0.08 yuan in general silver dollars), so long-term sentiment was greatly shaken, and prices gradually rose sharply. January to April all broke through the 0.03 yuan mark. According to recent observations of sentiment, there may still be opportunities for both near and far terms to continue to rise. The spot price in Tianjin decreased again, currently only 2.5 yuan. As a result, this month increased by 0.004 yuan compared to the previous day, December increased by 0.00425 yuan, January increased by 0.004 yuan, February increased by 0.00625 yuan, March increased by 0.00575 yuan, and April increased by 0.0055 yuan.

Wheat Jumps Up 0.08-0.09 Yuan

Yesterday's futures wheat market, after the morning opening, each month initially showed signs of consolidation. With foreign wheat quotations, decreasing by 0.03-0.04 yuan to 1.1 yuan, so sentiment was still flat at the opening. Then, due to very few sellers and still enthusiastic buyers, and with the flour market initially consolidating and then jumping, the market in each round was also shaken. This was partly because the underlying supply was not abundant and partly because there was a rumor that foreign wheat would have a mutual quota tax increase. In the current situation where domestic wheat is falling, sentiment is easily aroused. As a result, November and December each increased by 0.08 yuan, January increased by 0.07 yuan, February increased by 0.09 yuan, and March increased by 0.06 yuan. The current wheat market has few transactions, and prices are still stable. Medium and inferior goods also rose gradually, with Chongming wheat opening at 4.15 yuan, Liuhe wheat at 4.1 yuan, and Hankou wheat at 3.98 yuan, totaling 1,300 bales, reportedly handled by Xin Da.

Hexia Rice Continues to Fall by About 0.01 Yuan

(Hunan) Yesterday, the source of supply was over forty shops, totaling over five thousand stone. The purchase route has turned languid. Although the Tianjin, Qingdao, and Yantai gangs purchased over three thousand bales (nearly four thousand stone), the trend has been downstream. The vessels were fully loaded and departed gradually, causing buyers to temporarily hesitate. As a result, the market turned weak. Yesterday, late rice continued to soften by approximately 0.01 yuan. The purchase appetite for Changbang, Sutongbang, and Nangang japonica at the local shops was still average, and the market price only softened a few cents to about 0.01 yuan. Du Yang tip goods were lacking, but the situation was not as firm as before. Although the Yin Yuan liquor shops transported goods, the market was still flat.

(Hubei) Yesterday, over forty ships arrived from Hexia. Sales on the market remained sluggish. Sales opened largely flat, with new japonica premium goods flat, medium and inferior goods improving by several cents in the morning but falling back by about 0.01 yuan in the afternoon. Du Bu Ke tip goods remained flat, and Bai Yuan and Yin Yuan improved by several cents.

Peanuts Arrive in Large Quantities, Prices Fall by 0.10-0.20 Yuan

Since new peanuts entered the market, the market has become increasingly stable, causing the price of raw peanuts at the place of origin to fluctuate. Therefore, merchants are mainly engaged in transporting peanuts, so the supply has been quite large recently. Although the shops on the street have tried to sell as much as possible, sales are not as smooth as before. Yesterday, transactions still totaled over 3,000 bales, and prices decreased by 0.10-0.20 yuan.

Sugar Market: Refined White Sugar Improved by 0.05 Yuan

Yesterday, the sugar market was stable and unchanged. The guild set the price for 24 coarse sand white ordinary goods at 20.2 yuan. Lotus red and Taikoo sugar were unchanged, with little movement. The price of Zhenji's No. 1 white sugar from the local factory was 19 yuan, an increase of 0.05 yuan. No. 2 was 18.8 yuan, No. 3 was 8.6 yuan, and No. 4 was 18.4 yuan. It was heard that Zhonghua and Guohua factories had decided to close down due to the recent repeated decline in sugar prices and the competition from certain factories selling at low prices, resulting in heavy losses. With reduced production in the future, market prices may increase. Chen Chaoqing continued to be available, priced at 15.4 yuan.

Dried Goods: Old Dried Longans Arrive and are Sold Immediately

Only about 200 boxes of Quanzhou large dried longans arrived the day before yesterday. Due to recent low sales of new goods, most of this batch was old goods. Yesterday, most of them were sold, with the best quality priced at 45-46 yuan, followed by prices ranging from 32-33 yuan to around 10 yuan, trending flat.

Piece Goods: Suits and Overcoat Woolens Sell Well and are Firm

Since riding breeches and overcoats have become popular, Chinese-style overcoats have abandoned thick materials for thin ones. Therefore, the sales force of ordinary mass-market overcoat woolens has suddenly become sluggish. However, high-end pure wool suits and fancy woolens for Western clothing tailors still have strong purchase appetite, so their sales are still smooth. Black and white plaid and herringbone suit and overcoat woolens priced at over 10 yuan per yard have been selling well recently. Pure wool black and white plaid overcoat woolens at Friendship Company sell for 24 yuan per yard, while Japanese goods sell for 15 yuan. The trend is very active.

Urgent Relief Needed for Silk and Tea Industries

The Ministry of Industry is developing sales of Chinese silk to the United States, which has been the largest consumer of raw silk in the world. Our country's silk sales to the United States account for sixty percent of the total. However, after Japanese silk began to compete with low prices in the American market, Chinese silk sales slowed down. Now, they have plummeted. Silk prices have fallen drastically, and the silk industry is on the verge of bankruptcy. Silk industry associations in Jiangsu and Zhejiang are currently appealing to the government to find ways to provide relief. According to reliable sources from the Silk Control Committee, the Ministry of Industry has decided on a plan to develop sales of Chinese silk to the United States. It will establish a joint public-private association to promote Chinese silk sales to the United States, and actively implement the plan to rescue the silk industry and restore sales in the American market.

Last week, raw silk exports further decreased. Our country's exports of yellow and white raw silk further declined. Last week, only 669 bales were shipped to Europe and the United States, a decrease of 131 bales compared to the previous week.

The sales of rayon are unlikely to improve due to unstable foreign exchange rates. It is unlikely that sales of rayon to foreign buyers will improve. Yesterday, only 19 cases of "Double Star," "Triple Star," and "Flying Elephant" brand futures were purchased by silk weaving factories in this port. The prices ranged from 174.25 yuan to 170 yuan net, slightly lower than before.

The sales of plain white silk fabrics are also weakening. Although the labor strike in the New York dyeing and weaving factories is currently under mediation and resumption of work is expected, the silk factory workers are still insisting on their demands. There is now a backlog of silk, and consumption is still decreasing. Silk prices continue to weaken, and actual sales in Lyon remain sluggish. Silk factories are purchasing only as needed, and Japanese silk is being dumped aggressively. No one is asking about Chinese silk. Although inland silk merchants have some interest in plain white silk fabrics, they are relentlessly suppressing prices. Factories are selling off stock at a loss, with each bale losing around 200 yuan. Yesterday, 35 bales of plain white silk fabrics were purchased from silk factories in Hangzhou and Huzhou, and 10 bales of plain dried white silk fabrics were purchased from Zhonghe. Prices are trending downward.

Smooth Sales of Pingshui Pearl Tea to Europe

Yesterday, in the tea market of this port, Pingshui pearl tea from local merchants destined for Europe saw slightly smoother sales. A total of 270 boxes were purchased by Jardine Matheson and Tung Foo and other firms. High-grade tea sold for 90 to 96 yuan, while lower-grade tea sold for 77 yuan, a decrease of 10 yuan compared to previous prices. There were also sporadic negotiations for needle-shaped and precious eyebrow green teas from European and French firms, but no deals were made. Qimen black tea remained unsold.

Metals: Extremely Scarce Imports of English Tinplate

Although the trade in English tinplate has not been brisk recently, the stock in the market is very scarce. Therefore, the standard prices have been maintained and have not fallen. For example, 90-pound boxes are estimated at 15.8 yuan, 100-pound boxes at 17 yuan, double-sheet 90-pound boxes (i.e., 180 pounds) are estimated at 32 yuan, and 100-pound boxes (i.e., 200 pounds) are estimated at 34 yuan. However, recently, American goods have flooded the market, which has greatly impacted sales. However, overseas prices are very firm, with 90-pound boxes selling for 16 shillings, 100-pound boxes for 17 shillings and 8 pence, double-sheet 90-pound boxes for 32 shillings, and 100-pound boxes for 35 shillings and 6 pence. Moreover, the shilling exchange rate in this port is very high. Because there is no profit to be made, traders are not daring to purchase. Therefore, the arrival of English tinplate is particularly scarce, and there is a concern that the market may run out of stock in the future.
